### **Kategori 1.1: Jenis Website (13 Layanan)**

#### 1. **Landing Page / Profil Perusahaan**
- **Deskripsi:** Website 1 halaman berisi semua info bisnis dalam satu tampilan

SEWA BULANAN:

- Domain included (always)
- Hosting included (always)
- SSL included (always)
- Maintenance & support included
- Minor updates included

## üìù **PRICING STRUCTURE SUMMARY**

### **Standard Formula:**
```
BELI PUTUS = Rp 350,000/halaman (ownership 100%)
SEWA = Rp 150,000/halaman/bulan (all inclusive)

CUSTOM SERVICES = Quote based on complexity
```

### **Common Pricing:**
- Landing Page: Rp 350K (beli) / Rp 150K (sewa)
- Multi-page (5 hal): Rp 1.75jt (beli) / Rp 750K (sewa)
- E-commerce: Rp 3jt (beli) / Rp 1.3jt (sewa)
- Custom System: Mulai Rp 5jt
- Enterprise: Rp 15jt+

### **DIVISI 1: Website & Sistem** (35 layanan)
